| <span data-ttu-id="7abe3-1766">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7abe3-1766">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7abe3-1767">Valor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7abe3-1767">Value</span></span> |
